## TComponent

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Parent must be: *only inherited types can be placed*

TComponent is the father of all Tholos components. Super minimalistic, only defines few basic properties, methods and events.

### TComponent properties

Name

Type

Mandatory

Runtime

Hidden data

Default value

Ancestor

Description

**DevNote**

TEXT

No

No

No

Developer Note

**FunctionCode**

STRING

No

No

No

Function Code for Role management, use \# in case of function needs logged user only (without any role)

**Name**

STRING

Yes

No

Yes

Generic name

**NameSuffix**

STRING

No

No

No

Value of Name property will be suffixed with this value. Use ++ sign to concatenation, ex: "\_++@this.DBField.Value"

### TComponent events

Name

Type

Ancestor

Description

**onAfterInit**

PHP

[](javascript:jumpToDoc('');)

**onAfterRender**

PHP

[](javascript:jumpToDoc('');)

**onBeforeCreate**

PHP

[](javascript:jumpToDoc('');)

**onBeforeRender**

PHP

[](javascript:jumpToDoc('');)

### TComponent methods

Name

Ancestor

Description

**setDataParameters()**

[](javascript:jumpToDoc('');)

Sets data-dataparameters values. If previous values exist they will be merged.

------------------------------------------------------------------------

## TAction

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');) / [TAction](javascript:jumpToDoc('TAction');)

Parent must be: [TRoute](javascript:jumpToDoc('TRoute');)

TAction

### TAction properties

Name

Type

Mandatory

Runtime

Hidden data

Default value

Ancestor

Description

**DevNote**

TEXT

No

No

No

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Developer Note

**FunctionCode**

STRING

Yes

No

No

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Function Code for Role management, use \# in case of function needs logged user only (without any role)

**HTTPMethod**

STRING

No

No

Yes

HTTP method that the action will handle

**List of possible values**

    GET
    HEAD
    POST
    PUT
    DELETE
    TRACE
    OPTIONS
    CONNECT
    PATCH

**Name**

STRING

Yes

No

Yes

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Generic name

**NameSuffix**

STRING

No

No

No

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Value of Name property will be suffixed with this value. Use ++ sign to concatenation, ex: "\_++@this.DBField.Value"

**Page**

[TPage](javascript:jumpToDoc('TPage');)

No

No

No

**ResponseType**

STRING

Yes

No

Yes

HTML

Type of the generated response. HTML will render a full HTML5-compliant page while HTMLSnippet will only render a partial useful for AJAX page generators. JSON and PLAINTEXT are self-explanatory.

**List of possible values**

    HTML
    JSON
    JSONDATA
    PLAINTEXT
    XML
    NONE

### TAction events

Name

Type

Ancestor

Description

**onAfterInit**

PHP

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

**onAfterRender**

PHP

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

**onBeforeCreate**

PHP

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

**onBeforeRender**

PHP

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

### TAction methods

Name

Ancestor

Description

**navigate()**

[](javascript:jumpToDoc('');)

Navigate to this action

**setDataParameters()**

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Sets data-dataparameters values. If previous values exist they will be merged.

------------------------------------------------------------------------

## TCacheArrayItem

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');) / [TCacheArrayItem](javascript:jumpToDoc('TCacheArrayItem');)

Parent must be: [TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

TCacheArray stores rendered items in cache

### TCacheArrayItem properties

Name

Type

Mandatory

Runtime

Hidden data

Default value

Ancestor

Description

**CacheID**

STRING

Yes

No

No

Cache ID

**CacheInfo**

ARRAY

No

Yes

Yes

Cache info

**CacheRefresh**

BOOLEAN

No

Yes

Yes

Force cache to refresh

**CacheUsed**

BOOLEAN

No

Yes

Yes

Cache is used for reading data

**DevNote**

TEXT

No

No

No

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Developer Note

**IndexField**

[TDBField](javascript:jumpToDoc('TDBField');)

Yes

No

No

Field used as index in array

**Name**

STRING

Yes

No

No

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Generic name

**NameSuffix**

STRING

No

No

No

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Value of Name property will be suffixed with this value. Use ++ sign to concatenation, ex: "\_++@this.DBField.Value"

**OrderField**

[TDBField](javascript:jumpToDoc('TDBField');)

No

No

No

Render by its order value

**SyncField**

[TDBField](javascript:jumpToDoc('TDBField');)

No

No

No

Field that shows the record has been changed

### TCacheArrayItem events

Name

Type

Ancestor

Description

PHP

PHP

## TCacheArrayRenderer

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');) / [TCacheArrayRenderer](javascript:jumpToDoc('TCacheArrayRenderer');)

Parent must be: [TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

TCacheArrayRenderer - renders an array from the cache stored by a TCacheArray component

### TCacheArrayRenderer properties

Name

Type

Mandatory

Runtime

Hidden data

Default value

Ancestor

Description

**CacheID**

STRING

Yes

No

No

Cache ID

**CacheInfo**

ARRAY

No

Yes

No

Cache info

**CacheRefresh**

BOOLEAN

No

Yes

No

Force cache to refresh

**CacheSelectionMode**

STRING

Yes

No

No

All

**List of possible values**

    All
    NewItems
    NewOrModifiedItems
    ModifiedItems
    SyncedItems

**CacheUsed**

BOOLEAN

No

Yes

No

Cache is used for reading data

**DevNote**

TEXT

No

No

No

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Developer Note

**Enabled**

BOOLEAN

Yes

No

No

true

When true (default), control is enabled. Otherwise control is disabled.

**Name**

STRING

Yes

No

No

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Generic name

**NameSuffix**

STRING

No

No

No

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Value of Name property will be suffixed with this value. Use ++ sign to concatenation, ex: "\_++@this.DBField.Value"

**PurgeAt**

STRING

Yes

No

No

SameRenderPhase

**List of possible values**

    SameRenderPhase
    DifferentRenderPhase
    EveryRenderPhase
    Never

**PurgeNotRenderedItems**

BOOLEAN

Yes

No

No

false

In case it is true and an item is not rendered from the array it will be purged

**Sorting**

STRING

Yes

No

No

NONE

Order result by TCacheArrayItems OrderField value

**List of possible values**

    ASC
    DESC
    NONE

### TCacheArrayRenderer events

Name

Type

Ancestor

Description

**onAfterInit**

PHP

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

**onAfterRender**

PHP

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

**onBeforeCreate**

PHP

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

**onBeforeRender**

PHP

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

### TCacheArrayRenderer methods

Name

Ancestor

Description

**setDataParameters()**

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Sets data-dataparameters values. If previous values exist they will be merged.

Name

Type

Runtime

Hidden data

Default value

Ancestor

Description

**AJAXQueueID**

STRING

Yes

No

Yes

@this.Name

**Attributes**

TEXT

No

No

No

HTML Special attributes

Type

Mandatory

Runtime

Hidden data

Description

Yes

STRING

No

No

No

[TButton](javascript:jumpToDoc('TButton');)

    sm
    lg

**IconAlign**

STRING

No

No

No

left

[TButton](javascript:jumpToDoc('TButton');)

Alignment of the icon. Left means before the component's label or content, right means after it. Defaults to left.

**List of possible values**

    left
    right

STRING

No

No

Yes

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

### TDataProvider properties

Name

Type

Mandatory

Runtime

Hidden data

Default value

Ancestor

Description

**AutoOpenAllowed**

BOOLEAN

No

Yes

No

true

AutoOpen component between construct and render time. Defaults to false.

**CacheID**

STRING

Yes

No

No

@this.Name

Cache ID

**CacheInfo**

ARRAY

No

Yes

No

Cache info

**CacheMode**

STRING

Yes

No

No

ReadWrite

Cache access mode. In ReadWrite mode the component writes its result to the cache and reads it the next time it is opened. In WriteOnly mode the component always writes the cache, never reads it. In ReadOnly mode, the component always reads the cache, never writes.

**List of possible values**

    ReadWrite
    WriteOnly
    ReadOnly

**CachePartitionedBy**

STRING

No

No

No

The column name partitioning by. If empty the whole result will be cached, otherwise th result array will be cached in an indexed array with the first column.

**CachePartitionFilter**

[TQueryFilter](javascript:jumpToDoc('TQueryFilter');)

No

No

No

Cache partition parameter. If exists and cache is partitioned only the referenced index will be refreshed.

**CacheRefresh**

BOOLEAN

No

Yes

No

Force cache to refresh

**CacheSQLConflict**

STRING

No

No

No

What to do if the SQL stored in cache is different from the actual one

**List of possible values**

    ReadCache
    DisableCaching
    RewriteCache

**CacheUsed**

BOOLEAN

No

Yes

No

Cache is used for reading data

**CacheValidity**

NUMBER

No

No

No

Cache validity in minutes

**Caching**

STRING

Yes

No

**List of possible values**

    Disabled
    Private
    Shared

**DatabaseIndex**

NUMBER

No

No

No

Name

BOOLEAN

No

Yes

No

true

STRING

Yes

No

No

@this.Name

Cache ID

**CacheInfo**

ARRAY

No

Yes

No

[TDataProvider](javascript:jumpToDoc('TDataProvider');)

Cache info

**CacheMode**

STRING

Yes

No

No

ReadWrite

[TDataProvider](javascript:jumpToDoc('TDataProvider');)

Cache access mode. In ReadWrite mode the component writes its result to the cache and reads it the next time it is opened. In WriteOnly mode the component always writes the cache, never reads it. In ReadOnly mode, the component always reads the cache, never writes.

**List of possible values**

    ReadWrite
    WriteOnly
    ReadOnly

**CachePartitionedBy**

STRING

No

No

No

[TDataProvider](javascript:jumpToDoc('TDataProvider');)

The column name partitioning by. If empty the whole result will be cached, otherwise th result array will be cached in an indexed array with the first column.

**CachePartitionFilter**

[TQueryFilter](javascript:jumpToDoc('TQueryFilter');)

No

No

No

[TDataProvider](javascript:jumpToDoc('TDataProvider');)

Cache partition parameter. If exists and cache is partitioned only the referenced index will be refreshed.

**CacheRefresh**

BOOLEAN

No

Yes

No

[TDataProvider](javascript:jumpToDoc('TDataProvider');)

Force cache to refresh

**CacheSQLConflict**

STRING

Yes

No

No

DisableCaching

[TDataProvider](javascript:jumpToDoc('TDataProvider');)

What to do if the SQL stored in cache is different from the actual one

**CountTotalRows**

BOOLEAN

No

Yes

No

false

If true TQuery will count the total number of result before generating result. TotalRowCount property will hold the value. It may differ from RowCount property which is the number of rows given back after QueryLimit applied.

**CacheMode**

STRING

Yes

No

No

ReadWrite

[TDataProvider](javascript:jumpToDoc('TDataProvider');)

Cache access mode. In ReadWrite mode the component writes its result to the cache and reads it the next time it is opened. In WriteOnly mode the component always writes the cache, never reads it. In ReadOnly mode, the component always reads the cache, never writes.

**List of possible values**

    ReadWrite
    WriteOnly
    ReadOnly

**CacheRefresh**

BOOLEAN

No

Yes

No

[TDataProvider](javascript:jumpToDoc('TDataProvider');)

TTimer

### TTimer properties

Name

Type

Mandatory

Runtime

Hidden data

Default value

Ancestor

Description

**Async**

BOOLEAN

Yes

No

No

true

Asynchronus call. If false, it does not execute the onExecute trigger and waits RetryInterval msec before the next execution.

**AutoStart**

BOOLEAN

Yes

No

Yes

true

Start timer on document ready, otherwise Execute method must called manually.

**DevNote**

TEXT

No

No

No

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Developer Note

**Enabled**

BOOLEAN

Yes

No

Yes

true

When true (default), control is enabled. Otherwise control is disabled.

**EnabledOnActivate**

BOOLEAN

Yes

No

Yes

false

If true then activate() method overwrites enabled property to true. In other case enabled must be turned on manually before activates run.

**FunctionCode**

STRING

No

No

No

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Function Code for Role management, use \# in case of function needs logged user only (without any role)

**Interval**

NUMBER

Yes

No

No

5000

Interval in milliseconds

**Name**

STRING

Yes

No

Yes

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Generic name

**NameSuffix**

STRING

No

No

No

[TComponent](javascript:jumpToDoc('TComponent');)

Value of Name property will be suffixed with this value. Use ++ sign to concatenation, ex: "\_++@this.DBField.Value"

**RetryInterval**

NUMBER

Yes

No

No

100

RetryInterval in milliseconds in synchronous mode.

**StartInterval**

NUMBER

Yes

No

No

@this.Interval

First run

**TimerMode**

STRING

Yes

No

Yes

interval

interval: run in every Interval msec timeout: run once after Interval msec

**List of possible values**

    interval
    timeout

**WaitOnInactiveTab**

BOOLEAN

Yes

No

Yes

true
